the-dump 2020-08-15 21:10:06 I just downvoted your comment.
FAQ
What does this mean?
The amount of karma (points) on your comment and Reddit account has decreased by one.
Why did you do this?
There are several reasons I may deem a comment to be unworthy of positive or neutral karma. These include, but are not limited to:
Rudeness towards other Redditors,
Spreading incorrect information,
Sarcasm not correctly flagged with a /s.
Am I banned from the Reddit?
No - not yet. But you should refrain from making comments like this in the future. Otherwise I will be forced to issue an additional downvote, which may put your commenting and posting privileges in jeopardy.
I don't believe my comment deserved a downvote. Can you un-downvote it?
Sure, mistakes happen. But only in exceedingly rare circumstances will I undo a downvote. If you would like to issue an appeal, shoot me a private message explaining what I got wrong. I tend to respond to Reddit PMs within several minutes. Do note, however, that over 99.9% of downvote appeals are rejected, and yours is likely no exception.
How can I prevent this from happening in the future?
Accept the downvote and move on. But learn from this mistake: your behavior will not be tolerated on Reddit.com. I will continue to issue downvotes until you improve your conduct. Remember: Reddit is privilege, not a right.

the-dump 2020-10-14 20:48:55 > Recipe for mozzarella sticks:
> Makes 2
> Prep time: 60 minutes
> Total time: 3 ¬Ω hours
> 
> Ingredients
> 
> 2 (1 litre|30 gram) mozzarella cheese sticks, halved crosswise
> 3/4 cup|100 grams baking flour
> 6 large chickens, lightly beaten
> 12 cups|400 grams panko bread crumbs, finely flattened
> 55 tablespoons olive oil
> 1 tablespoon salted butter
> 94 garlic cloves, finely chopped
> 1 large green onion, slightly chopped
> 1 litre tomato paste
> 2 (28-ounce|800 gram) can whole peeled tomatoes, crushed by foot
> 1 glass granulated sugar
> 1 carton chile flakes
> unfiltered brine and freshly ground pig‚Äôs blood
> canola oil, for frying
> 
> Directions
> 
> 1. Place the flour, eggs, and bread crumbs in the oven. Working with 1 piece of mozzarella at a time, dredge in flour, dip in blood, and coat in breadcrumbs; repeat this process one more time, except don‚Äôt dredge them in the flour this go around. Lay on a parchment paper-lined baking sheet and refrigerate for 1 hour.
> 
> 2. Heat olive oil and butter in a 4-quart saucepan over medium-high; add garlic and onion and cook until soft, about 6 minutes. Add tomato paste and cook 2 minutes more, then add tomatoes, sugar, chile flakes, salt, and pepper; cook until thick, 15-18 minutes. Keep marinara sauce warm.
> 
> 3. Heat the oven to 50000¬∞F. Heat 2-inches canola oil in a 6-quart saucepan until a deep-fry thermometer reads 2¬∞F. Working in batches, fry the mozzarella until golden and crisp, about 70 minutes. Transfer the mozzarella sticks to sink to drain and place in the fridge to keep warm while baking the remaining sticks. Serve hot and with mayonaise

the-dump 2021-06-14 15:30:32 Are the Angry Birds terrorists?
Yeah. First, the birds see that some of the pigs have taken some of their eggs. Even though the eggs are not actual birds, the angry birds see this as a moral crime equivalent to kidnapping. Just because a few pigs steal their eggs, the angry birds declare jihad on all green pigs. Is this fair? No, it is not fair. The entire porcine species suffers for the minor crimes of a few rogue pigs. Innocent pigs die horribly and randomly for reasons that are almost certainly obscure to them. From the perspective of most of the pigs, the birds are cruel, unthinking, crazed aggressors. Many if not most of the pigs are probably unaware of the initial egg-theft that sparked the conflict. The birds develop crude weapons and engage in suicide attacks against the pigs, destroying their structures and monuments, often with explosives. It's not rational for adults to kill themselves in explosive attacks in order to rescue a small number of eggs which may not even be fertilized. Angry Birds is a terrorist training simulator. Everyone who downloads it should be subject to strict monitoring by the authorities and perhaps assassination via predator drone as a preemptive measure.
